Task instruction sent to agent 
# big-code-k8s-bug-001: Missing ResourceSlice Event Handler in Kubernetes Scheduler

## Task

Investigate a bug in the Kubernetes scheduler where pods requesting Dynamic Resource Allocation (DRA) devices become permanently stuck in an Unschedulable state when the DRA driver starts after the pod is created. Trace the execution path through the scheduler's event-driven re-queuing architecture to identify why ResourceSlice creation/update events are silently dropped.

## Context

- **Repository**: kubernetes/kubernetes (Go, ~3.5M LOC)
- **Category**: Bug Investigation
- **Difficulty**: hard
- **Entry Point**: `pkg/scheduler/schedule_one.go` — `ScheduleOne()` method

## Symptom

When a pod requests a DRA device and the DRA driver starts *after* the pod is created, the pod becomes permanently stuck in `Pending` with reason `Unschedulable`. The scheduler logs `"cannot allocate all claims"` because no ResourceSlices exist at scheduling time. After the driver starts and publishes ResourceSlice objects, the pod should be rescheduled — but it never is.

The bug is a race condition: if the driver starts first, scheduling succeeds immediately. But if the pod arrives before the driver, the scheduler never retries because ResourceSlice events are not wired into the scheduling queue's re-evaluation mechanism.

## Requirements

1. Starting from the entry point, trace the execution path to the root cause
2. Identify the specific file(s) and line(s) where the bug originates
3. Explain WHY the bug occurs — focus on the event handler registration mechanism and the scheduling queue's re-evaluation trigger
4. Propose a fix with specific code changes

## Expected Output

Write your analysis to `/logs/agent/solution.md` with the following structure:

```

## Evaluation Criteria

- Root cause identification: Did you find the correct file(s) where the bug originates?
- Call chain accuracy: Did you trace the correct path from symptom to root cause?
- Fix quality: Is the proposed fix correct and minimal?

func (pl *dynamicResources) EventsToRegister() []framework.ClusterEventWithHint {

type FailureHandlerFn func(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, podInfo *framework.QueuedPodInfo, status *framework.Status, nominatingInfo *framework.NominatingInfo, start time.Time)

func unionedGVKs(queueingHintsPerProfile internalqueue.QueueingHintMapPerProfile) map[framework.GVK]framework.ActionType {
	gvkMap := make(map[framework.GVK]framework.ActionType)
	for _, queueingHints := range queueingHintsPerProfile {
		for evt := range queueingHints {
			if _, ok := gvkMap[evt.Resource]; ok {
				gvkMap[evt.Resource] |= evt.ActionType
			} else {
				gvkMap[evt.Resource] = evt.ActionType
			}
		}
	}
	return gvkMap
}

85-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've completed the investigation and written a comprehensive analysis. Let me show you a summary:

## Summary

I've successfully traced the Kubernetes scheduler bug where pods requesting Dynamic Resource Allocation (DRA) devices become permanently stuck in `Unschedulable` state. Here's what I found:

### **Root Cause**
The bug occurs due to **missing ResourceSlice event handler registration** across three interconnected components:

1. **`pkg/scheduler/framework/types.go`** (lines 68-106)
   - Missing `ResourceSlice GVK` constant definition
   - Missing `ResourceSlice` from `UnrollWildCardResource()` function

2. **`pkg/scheduler/eventhandlers.go`** (lines 395-543)
   - Missing `case framework.ResourceSlice:` in the event handler registration switch statement
   - No handler to attach to the ResourceSlice informer

3. **`pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/dynamicresources/dynamicresources.go`** (lines 381-412)
   - Plugin's `EventsToRegister()` method does NOT include ResourceSlice events
   - Despite using `ResourceSliceLister`, the plugin never requests event notifications

### **Why It Causes the Bug**
1. Pod arrives → dynamicresources plugin sees no ResourceSlices → marks pod `Unschedulable`
2. Pod is added to unschedulable queue awaiting a re-evaluation event
3. DRA driver publishes ResourceSlices
4. **No event handler exists to catch ResourceSlice changes** → Event is silently dropped
5. Pod remains stuck forever waiting for an event that will never trigger

### **The Fix** (4 Changes)
1. Add `ResourceSlice GVK = "ResourceSlice"` to `framework/types.go`
2. Add ResourceSlice to `UnrollWildCardResource()` in `framework/types.go`
3. Add ResourceSlice case to event handler registration in `eventhandlers.go`
4. Add ResourceSlice events to plugin's `EventsToRegist
... (truncated)

of the assumption step above).\n\tgo func() {\n\t\tbindingCycleCtx, cancel := context.WithCancel(ctx)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t\tmetrics.Goroutines.WithLabelValues(metrics.Binding).Inc()\n\t\tdefer metrics.Goroutines.WithLabelValues(metrics.Binding).Dec()\n\n\t\tstatus := sched.bindingCycle(bindingCycleCtx, state, fwk, scheduleResult, assumedPodInfo, start, podsToActivate)\n\t\tif !status.IsSuccess() {\n\t\t\tsched.handleBindingCycleError(bindingCycleCtx, state, fwk, assumedPodInfo, start, scheduleResult, status)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Usually, DonePod is called inside the scheduling queue,\n\t\t// but in this case, we need to call it here because this Pod won't go back to the scheduling queue.\n\t\tsched.SchedulingQueue.Done(assumedPodInfo.Pod.UID)\n\t}()\n}\n\nvar clearNominatedNode = &framework.NominatingInfo{NominatingMode: framework.ModeOverride, NominatedNodeName: \"\"}\n\n// schedulingCycle tries to schedule a single Pod.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) schedulingCycle(\n\tctx context.Context,\n\tstate *framework.CycleState,\n\tfwk framework.Framework,\n\tpodInfo *framework.QueuedPodInfo,\n\tstart time.Time,\n\tpodsToActivate *framework.PodsToActivate,\n) (ScheduleResult, *framework.QueuedPodInfo, *framework.Status) {\n\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n\tpod := podInfo.Pod\n\tscheduleResult, err := sched.SchedulePod(ctx, fwk, state, pod)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tdefer func() {\n\t\t\tmetrics.SchedulingAlgorithmLatency.Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(start))\n\t\t}()\n\t\tif err == ErrNoNodesAvailable {\n\t\t\tstatus := framework.NewStatus(framework.UnschedulableAndUnresolvable).WithError(err)\n\t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, podInfo, status\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfitError, ok := err.(*framework.FitError)\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Error selecting node for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n\t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, podInfo, framework.AsStatus(err)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// SchedulePod() may have failed because the pod would not fit on any host, so we try to\n\t\t// preempt, with the expectation that the next time the pod is tried for scheduling it\n\t\t// will fit due to the preemption. It is also possible that a different pod will schedule\n\t\t// into the resources that were preempted, but this is harmless.\n\n\t\tif !fwk.HasPostFilterPlugins() {\n\t\t\tlogger.V(3).Info(\"No PostFilter plugins are registered, so no preemption will be performed\")\n\t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{}, podInfo, framework.NewStatus(framework.Unschedulable).WithError(err)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Run PostFilter plugins to attempt to make the pod schedulable in a future scheduling cycle.\n\t\tresult, status := fwk.RunPostFilterPlugins(ctx, state, pod, fitError.Diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap)\n\t\tmsg := status.Message()\n\t\tfitError.Diagnosis.PostFilterMsg = msg\n\t\tif status.Code() == framework.Error {\n\t\t\tlogger.Error(nil, \"Status after running PostFilter plugins for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"status\", msg)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Status after running PostFilter plugins for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"status\", msg)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar nominatingInfo *framework.NominatingInfo\n\t\tif result != nil {\n\t\t\tnominatingInfo = result.NominatingInfo\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: nominatingInfo}, podInfo, framework.NewStatus(framework.Unschedulable).WithError(err)\n\t}\n\n\tmetrics.SchedulingAlgorithmLatency.Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(start))\n\t// Tell the cache to assume that a pod now is running on a given node, even though it hasn't been bound yet.\n\t// This allows us to keep scheduling without waiting on binding to occur.\n\tassumedPodInfo := podInfo.DeepCopy()\n\tassumedPod := assumedPodInfo.Pod\n\t// assume modifies `assumedPod` by setting NodeName=scheduleResult.SuggestedHost\n\terr = sched.assume(logger, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\t// This is most probably result of a BUG in retrying logic.\n\t\t// We report an error here so that pod scheduling can be retried.\n\t\t// This relies on the fact that Error will check if the pod has been bound\n\t\t// to a node and if so will not add it back to the unscheduled pods queue\n\t\t// (otherwise this would cause an infinite loop).\n\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, framework.AsStatus(err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Run the Reserve method of reserve plugins.\n\tif sts := fwk.RunReservePluginsReserve(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost); !sts.IsSuccess() {\n\t\t// trigger un-reserve to clean up state associated with the reserved Pod\n\t\tfwk.RunReservePluginsUnreserve(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n\t\tif forgetErr := sched.Cache.ForgetPod(logger, assumedPod); forgetErr != nil {\n\t\t\tlogger.Error(forgetErr, \"Scheduler cache ForgetPod failed\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif sts.IsRejected() {\n\t\t\tfitErr := &framework.FitError{\n\t\t\t\tNumAllNodes: 1,\n\t\t\t\tPod:         pod,\n\t\t\t\tDiagnosis: framework.Diagnosis{\n\t\t\t\t\tNodeToStatusMap: framework.NodeToStatusMap{scheduleResult.SuggestedHost: sts},\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfitErr.Diagnosis.AddPluginStatus(sts)\n\t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, framework.NewStatus(sts.Code()).WithError(fitErr)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, sts\n\t}\n\n\t// Run \"permit\" plugins.\n\trunPermitStatus := fwk.RunPermitPlugins(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n\tif !runPermitStatus.IsWait() && !runPermitStatus.IsSuccess() {\n\t\t// trigger un-reserve to clean up state associated with the reserved Pod\n\t\tfwk.RunReservePluginsUnreserve(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n\t\tif forgetErr := sched.Cache.ForgetPod(logger, assumedPod); forgetErr != nil {\n\t\t\tlogger.Error(forgetErr, \"Scheduler cache ForgetPod failed\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif runPermitStatus.IsRejected() {\n\t\t\tfitErr := &framework.FitError{\n\t\t\t\tNumAllNodes: 1,\n\t\t\t\tPod:         pod,\n\t\t\t\tDiagnosis: framework.Diagnosis{\n\t\t\t\t\tNodeToStatusMap: framework.NodeToStatusMap{scheduleResult.SuggestedHost: runPermitStatus},\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfitErr.Diagnosis.AddPluginStatus(runPermitStatus)\n\t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, framework.NewStatus(runPermitStatus.Code()).WithError(fitErr)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, runPermitStatus\n\t}\n\n\t// At the end of a successful scheduling cycle, pop and move up Pods if needed.\n\tif len(podsToActivate.Map) != 0 {\n\t\tsched.SchedulingQueue.Activate(logger, podsToActivate.Map)\n\t\t// Clear the entries after activation.\n\t\tpodsToActivate.Map = make(map[string]*v1.Pod)\n\t}\n\n\treturn scheduleResult, assumedPodInfo, nil\n}\n\n// bindingCycle tries to bind an assumed Pod.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) bindingCycle(\n\tctx context.Context,\n\tstate *framework.CycleState,\n\tfwk framework.Framework,\n\tscheduleResult ScheduleResult,\n\tassumedPodInfo *framework.QueuedPodInfo,\n\tstart time.Time,\n\tpodsToActivate *framework.PodsToActivate) *framework.Status {\n\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n\n\tassumedPod := assumedPodInfo.Pod\n\n\t// Run \"permit\" plugins.\n\tif status := fwk.WaitOnPermit(ctx, assumedPod); !status.IsSuccess() {\n\t\tif status.IsRejected() {\n\t\t\tfitErr := &framework.FitError{\n\t\t\t\tNumAllNodes: 1,\n\t\t\t\tPod:         assumedPodInfo.Pod,\n\t\t\t\tDiagnosis: framework.Diagnosis{\n\t\t\t\t\tNodeToStatusMap:      framework.NodeToStatusMap{scheduleResult.SuggestedHost: status},\n\t\t\t\t\tUnschedulablePlugins: sets.New(status.Plugin()),\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn framework.NewStatus(status.Code()).WithError(fitErr)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn status\n\t}\n\n\t// Run \"prebind\" plugins.\n\tif status := fwk.RunPreBindPlugins(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost); !status.IsSuccess() {\n\t\treturn status\n\t}\n\n\t// Run \"bind\" plugins.\n\tif status := sched.bind(ctx, fwk, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost, state); !status.IsSuccess() {\n\t\treturn status\n\t}\n\n\t// Calculating nodeResourceString can be heavy. Avoid it if klog verbosity is below 2.\n\tlogger.V(2).Info(\"Successfully bound pod to node\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(assumedPod), \"node\", scheduleResult.SuggestedHost, \"evaluatedNodes\", scheduleResult.EvaluatedNodes, \"feasibleNodes\", scheduleResult.FeasibleNodes)\n\tmetrics.PodScheduled(fwk.ProfileName(), metrics.SinceInSeconds(start))\n\tmetrics.PodSchedulingAttempts.Observe(float64(assumedPodInfo.Attempts))\n\tif assumedPodInfo.InitialAttemptTimestamp != nil {\n\t\tmetrics.PodSchedulingDuration.WithLabelValues(getAttemptsLabel(assumedPodInfo)).Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(*assumedPodInfo.InitialAttemptTimestamp))\n\t\tmetrics.PodSchedulingSLIDuration.WithLabelValues(getAttemptsLabel(assumedPodInfo)).Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(*assumedPodInfo.InitialAttemptTimestamp))\n\t}\n\t// Run \"postbind\" plugins.\n\tfwk.RunPostBindPlugins(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n\n\t// At the end of a successful binding cycle, move up Pods if needed.\n\tif len(podsToActivate.Map) != 0 {\n\t\tsched.SchedulingQueue.Activate(logger, podsToActivate.Map)\n\t\t// Unlike the logic in schedulingCycle(), we don't bother deleting the entries\n\t\t// as `podsToActivate.Map` is no longer consumed.\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) handleBindingCycleError(\n\tctx context.Context,\n\tstate *framework.CycleState,\n\tfwk framework.Framework,\n\tpodInfo *framework.QueuedPodInfo,\n\tstart time.Time,\n\tscheduleResult ScheduleResult,\n\tstatus *framework.Status) {\n\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n\n\tassumedPod := podInfo.Pod\n\t// trigger un-reserve plugins to clean up state associated with the reserved Pod\n\tfwk.RunReservePluginsUnreserve(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n\tif forgetErr := sched.Cache.ForgetPod(logger, assumedPod); forgetErr != nil {\n\t\tlogger.Error(forgetErr, \"scheduler cache ForgetPod failed\")\n\t} else {\n\t\t// \"Forget\"ing an assumed Pod in binding cycle should be treated as a PodDelete event,\n\t\t// as the assumed Pod had occupied a certain amount of resources in scheduler cache.\n\t\t//\n\t\t// Avoid moving the assumed Pod itself as it's always Unschedulable.\n\t\t// It's intentional to \"defer\" this operation; otherwise MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue() would\n\t\t// add this event to in-flight events and thus move the assumed pod to backoffQ anyways if the plugins don't have appropriate QueueingHint.\n\t\tif status.IsRejected() {\n\t\t\tdefer sched.SchedulingQueue.MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue(logger, internalqueue.AssignedPodDelete, assumedPod, nil, func(pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n\t\t\t\treturn assumedPod.UID != pod.UID\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tsched.SchedulingQueue.MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue(logger, internalqueue.AssignedPodDelete, assumedPod, nil, nil)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tsched.FailureHandler(ctx, fwk, podInfo, status, clearNominatedNode, start)\n}\n\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) frameworkForPod(pod *v1.Pod) (framework.Framework, error) {\n\tfwk, ok := sched.Profiles[pod.Spec.SchedulerName]\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"profile not found for scheduler name %q\", pod.Spec.SchedulerName)\n\t}\n\treturn fwk, nil\n}\n\n// skipPodSchedule returns true if we could skip scheduling the pod for specified cases.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) skipPodSchedule(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n\t// Case 1: pod is being deleted.\n\tif pod.DeletionTimestamp != nil {\n\t\tfwk.EventRecorder().Eventf(pod, nil, v1.EventTypeWarning, \"FailedScheduling\", \"Scheduling\", \"skip schedule deleting pod: %v/%v\", pod.Namespace, pod.Name)\n\t\tklog.FromContext(ctx).V(3).Info(\"Skip schedule deleting pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\n\t// Case 2: pod that has been assumed could be skipped.\n\t// An assumed pod can be added again to the scheduling queue if it got an update event\n\t// during its previous scheduling cycle but before getting assumed.\n\tisAssumed, err := sched.Cache.IsAssumedPod(pod)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\t// TODO(91633): pass ctx into a revised HandleError\n\t\tutilruntime.HandleError(fmt.Errorf(\"failed to check whether pod %s/%s is assumed: %v\", pod.Namespace, pod.Name, err))\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\treturn isAssumed\n}\n\n// schedulePod tries to schedule the given pod to one of the nodes in the node list.\n// If it succeeds, it will return the name of the node.\n// If it fails, it will return a FitError with reasons.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) schedulePod(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, state *framework.CycleState, pod *v1.Pod) (result ScheduleResult, err error) {\n\ttrace := utiltrace.New(\"Scheduling\", utiltrace.Field{Key: \"namespace\", Value: pod.Namespace}, utiltrace.Field{Key: \"name\", Value: pod.Name})\n\tdefer trace.LogIfLong(100 * time.Millisecond)\n\tif err := sched.Cache.UpdateSnapshot(klog.FromContext(ctx), sched.nodeInfoSnapshot); err != nil {\n\t\treturn result, err\n\t}\n\ttrace.Step(\"Snapshotting scheduler cache and node infos done\")\n\n\tif sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.NumNodes() == 0 {\n\t\treturn result, ErrNoNodesAvailable\n\t}\n\n\tfeasibleNodes, diagnosis, err := sched.findNodesThatFitPod(ctx, fwk, state, pod)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn result, err\n\t}\n\ttrace.Step(\"Computing predicates done\")\n\n\tif len(feasibleNodes) == 0 {\n\t\treturn result, &framework.FitError{\n\t\t\tPod:         pod,\n\t\t\tNumAllNodes: sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.NumNodes(),\n\t\t\tDiagnosis:   diagnosis,\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// When only one node after predicate, just use it.\n\tif len(feasibleNodes) == 1 {\n\t\treturn ScheduleResult{\n\t\t\tSuggestedHost:  feasibleNodes[0].Node().Name,\n\t\t\tEvaluatedNodes: 1 + len(diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap),\n\t\t\tFeasibleNodes:  1,\n\t\t}, nil\n\t}\n\n\tpriorityList, err := prioritizeNodes(ctx, sched.Extenders, fwk, state, pod, feasibleNodes)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn result, err\n\t}\n\n\thost, _, err := selectHost(priorityList, numberOfHighestScoredNodesToReport)\n\ttrace.Step(\"Prioritizing done\")\n\n\treturn ScheduleResult{\n\t\tSuggestedHost:  host,\n\t\tEvaluatedNodes: len(feasibleNodes) + len(diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap),\n\t\tFeasibleNodes:  len(feasibleNodes),\n\t}, err\n}\n\n// Filters the nodes to find the ones that fit the pod based on the framework\n// filter plugins and filter extenders.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) findNodesThatFitPod(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, state *framework.CycleState, pod *v1.Pod) ([]*framework.NodeInfo, framework.Diagnosis, error) {\n\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n\tdiagnosis := framework.Diagnosis{\n\t\tNodeToStatusMap: make(framework.NodeToStatusMap),\n\t}\n\n\tallNodes, err := sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.NodeInfos().List()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, err\n\t}\n\t// Run \"prefilter\" plugins.\n\tpreRes, s := fwk.RunPreFilterPlugins(ctx, state, pod)\n\tif !s.IsSuccess() {\n\t\tif !s.IsRejected() {\n\t\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, s.AsError()\n\t\t}\n\t\t// All nodes in NodeToStatusMap will have the same status so that they can be handled in the preemption.\n\t\t// Some non trivial refactoring is needed to avoid this copy.\n\t\tfor _, n := range allNodes {\n\t\t\tdiagnosis.NodeToStatusMap[n.Node().Name] = s\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Record the messages from PreFilter in Diagnosis.PreFilterMsg.\n\t\tmsg := s.Message()\n\t\tdiagnosis.PreFilterMsg = msg\n\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Status after running PreFilter plugins for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"status\", msg)\n\t\tdiagnosis.AddPluginStatus(s)\n\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// \"NominatedNodeName\" can potentially be set in a previous scheduling cycle as a result of preemption.\n\t// This node is likely the only candidate that will fit the pod, and hence we try it first before iterating over all nodes.\n\tif len(pod.Status.NominatedNodeName) > 0 {\n\t\tfeasibleNodes, err := sched.evaluateNominatedNode(ctx, pod, fwk, state, diagnosis)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Evaluation failed on nominated node\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"node\", pod.Status.NominatedNodeName)\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Nominated node passes all the filters, scheduler is good to assign this node to the pod.\n\t\tif len(feasibleNodes) != 0 {\n\t\t\treturn feasibleNodes, diagnosis, nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tnodes := allNodes\n\tif !preRes.AllNodes() {\n\t\tnodes = make([]*framework.NodeInfo, 0, len(preRes.NodeNames))\n\t\tfor _, n := range allNodes {\n\t\t\tif !preRes.NodeNames.Has(n.Node().Name) {\n\t\t\t\t// We consider Nodes that are filtered out by PreFilterResult as rejected via UnschedulableAndUnresolvable.\n\t\t\t\t// We have to record them in NodeToStatusMap so that they won't be considered as candidates in the preemption.\n\t\t\t\tdiagnosis.NodeToStatusMap[n.Node().Name] = framework.NewStatus(framework.UnschedulableAndUnresolvable, \"node is filtered out by the prefilter result\")\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tnodes = append(nodes, n)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tfeasibleNodes, err := sched.findNodesThatPassFilters(ctx, fwk, state, pod, &diagnosis, nodes)\n\t// always try to update the sched.nextStartNodeIndex regardless of whether an error has occurred\n\t// this is helpful to make sure that all the nodes have a chance to be searched\n\tprocessedNodes := len(feasibleNodes) + len(diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap)\n\tsched.nextStartNodeIndex = (sched.nextStartNodeIndex + processedNodes) % len(nodes)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, err\n\t}\n\n\tfeasibleNodesAfterExtender, err := findNodesThatPassExtenders(ctx, sched.Extenders, pod, feasibleNodes, diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, err\n\t}\n\tif len(feasibleNodesAfterExtender) != len(feasibleNodes) {\n\t\t// Extenders filtered out some nodes.\n\t\t//\n\t\t// Extender doesn't support any kind of requeueing feature like EnqueueExtensions in the scheduling framework.\n\t\t// When Extenders reject some Nodes and the pod ends up being unschedulable,\n\t\t// we put framework.ExtenderName to pInfo.UnschedulablePlugins.\n\t\t// This Pod will be requeued from unschedulable pod pool to activeQ/backoffQ\n\t\t// by any kind of cluster events.\n\t\t// https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/122019\n\t\tif diagnosis.UnschedulablePlugins == nil {\n\t\t\tdiagnosis.UnschedulablePlugins = sets.New[string]()\n\t\t}\n\t\tdiagnosis.UnschedulablePlugins.Insert(framework.ExtenderName)\n\t}\n\n\treturn feasibleNodesAfterExtender, diagnosis, nil\n}\n\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) evaluateNominatedNode(ctx context.Context, pod *v1.Pod, fwk framework.Framework, state *framework.CycleState, diagnosis framework.Diagnosis) ([]*framework.NodeInfo, error) {\n\tnnn := pod.Status.NominatedNodeName\n\tnodeInfo, err := sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.Get(nnn)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tnode := []*framework.NodeInfo{nodeInfo}\n\tfeasibleNodes, err := sched.findNodesThatPassFilters(ctx, fwk, state, pod, &diagnosis, node)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tfeasibleNodes, err = findNodesThatPassExtenders(ctx, sched.Extenders, pod, feasibleNodes, diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\treturn feasibleNodes, nil\n}\n\n// hasScoring checks if scoring nodes is configured.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) hasScoring(fwk framework.Framework) bool {\n\tif fwk.HasScorePlugins() {\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\tfor _, extender := range sched.Extenders {\n\t\tif extender.IsPrioritizer() {\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn false\n}\n\n// hasExtenderFilters checks if any extenders filter nodes.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) hasExtenderFilters() bool {\n\tfor _, extender := range sched.Extenders {\n\t\tif extender.IsFilter() {\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn false\n}\n\n// findNodesThatPassFilters finds the nodes that fit the filter plugins.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) findNodesThatPassFilters(\n\tctx context.Context,\n\tfwk framework.Framework,\n\tstate *framework.CycleState,\n\tpod *v1.Pod,\n\tdiagnosis *framework.Diagnosis,\n\tnodes []*framework.NodeInfo) ([]*framework.NodeInfo, error) {\n\tnumAllNodes := len(nodes)\n\tnumNodesToFind := sched.numFeasibleNodesToFind(fwk.PercentageOfNodesToScore(), int32(numAllNodes))\n\tif !sched.hasExtenderFilters() && !sched.hasScoring(fwk) {\n\t\tnumNodesToFind = 1\n\t}\n\n\t// Create feasible list with enough space to avoid growing it\n\t// and allow assigning.\n\tfeasibleNodes := make([]*framework.NodeInfo, numNodesToFind)\n\n\tif !fwk.HasFilterPlugins() {\n\t\tfor i := range feasibleNodes {\n\t\t\tfeasibleNodes[i] = nodes[(sched.nextStartNodeIndex+i)%numAllNodes]\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn feasibleNodes, nil\n\t}\n\n\terrCh := parallelize.NewErrorChannel()\n\tvar feasibleNodesLen int32\n\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(ctx)\n\tdefer cancel()\n\n\ttype nodeStatus struct {\n\t\tnode   string\n\t\tstatus *framework.Status\n\t}\n\tresult := make([]*nodeStatus, numAllNodes)\n\tcheckNode := func(i int) {\n\t\t// We check the nodes starting from where we left off in the previous scheduling cycle,\n\t\t// this is to make sure all nodes have the same chance of being examined across pods.\n\t\tnodeInfo := nodes[(sched.nextStartNodeIndex+i)%numAllNodes]\n\t\tstatus := fwk.RunFilterPluginsWithNominatedPods(ctx, state, pod, nodeInfo)\n\t\tif status.Code() == framework.Error {\n\t\t\terrCh.SendErrorWithCancel(status.AsError(), cancel)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tif status.IsSuccess() {\n\t\t\tlength := atomic.AddInt32(&feasibleNodesLen, 1)\n\t\t\tif length > numNodesToFind {\n\t\t\t\tcancel()\n\t\t\t\tatomic.AddInt32(&feasibleNodesLen, -1)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tfeasibleNodes[length-1] = nodeInfo\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tresult[i] = &nodeStatus{node: nodeInfo.Node().Name, status: status}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tbeginCheckNode := time.Now()\n\tstatusCode := framework.Success\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\t// We record Filter extension point latency here instead of in framework.go because framework.RunFilterPlugins\n\t\t// function is called for each node, whereas we want to have an overall latency for all nodes per scheduling cycle.\n\t\t// Note that this latency also includes latency for `addNominatedPods`, which calls framework.RunPreFilterAddPod.\n\t\tmetrics.FrameworkExtensionPointDuration.WithLabelValues(metrics.Filter, statusCode.String(), fwk.ProfileName()).Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(beginCheckNode))\n\t}()\n\n\t// Stops searching for more nodes once the configured number of feasible nodes\n\t// are found.\n\tfwk.Parallelizer().Until(ctx, numAllNodes, checkNode, metrics.Filter)\n\tfeasibleNodes = feasibleNodes[:feasibleNodesLen]\n\tfor _, item := range result {\n\t\tif item == nil extenders are run as well.\n// All scores are finally combined (added) to get the total weighted scores of all nodes\nfunc prioritizeNodes(\n\tctx context.Context,\n\textenders           { return len(h) }\nfunc (h nodeScoreHeap) Less(i, j int) bool { return h[i].TotalScore > h[j].TotalScore }\nfunc (h nodeScoreHeap) Swap(i, j int)      { h[i], h[j] = h[j], h[i] }\n\nfunc (h 323\u2192\n   324\u2192func (sched *Scheduler) handleBindingCycleError(\n   325\u2192\tctx context.Context,\n   326\u2192\tstate *framework.CycleState,\n   327\u2192\tfwk framework.Framework,\n 338\u2192\t\tlogger.Error(forgetErr, \"scheduler cache ForgetPod failed\")\n   339\u2192\t} else {\n   340\u2192\t\t// \"Forget\"ing an assumed Pod in binding cycle should be treated as a PodDelete event,\n   341\u2192\t\t// as the assumed Pod had occupied a certain amount of resources in scheduler cache.\n   342\u2192\t\t//\n   343\u2192\t\t// Avoid moving the assumed Pod itself as it's always scheduling the pod for specified cases.\n   367\u2192func (sched *Scheduler) skipPodSchedule(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n   368\u2192\t// Case 1: pod is being deleted.\n   369\u2192\tif pod.DeletionTimestamp != nil {\n   370\u2192\t\tfwk.EventRecorder().Eventf(pod, nil, v1.EventTypeWarning, \"FailedScheduling\", \"Scheduling\", \"skip schedule deleting pod: 383\u2192\t}\n   384\u2192\treturn isAssumed\n   385\u2192}\n   386\u2192\n   387\u2192// schedulePod tries to schedule the given pod to one of the nodes in the node list.\n   388\u2192// If it succeeds, it will return the name of the node.\n   389\u2192// If it fails, it will return a FitError with reasons.\n   390\u2192func (sched *Scheduler) schedulePod(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, state *framework.CycleState, pod *v1.Pod) (result ScheduleResult, err error) {\n   391\u2192\ttrace := utiltrace.New(\"Scheduling\", utiltrace.Field{Key: \"namespace\", Value: pod.Namespace}, utiltrace.Field{Key: \"name\", Value: pod.Name})\n   392\u2192\tdefer trace.LogIfLong(100 * time.Millisecond)\n   393\u2192\tif err := sched.Cache.UpdateSnapshot(klog.FromContext(ctx), sched.nodeInfoSnapshot); err != nil {\n   394\u2192\t\treturn result, err\n   395\u2192\t}\n   396\u2192\ttrace.Step(\"Snapshotting scheduler cache and node infos done\")\n   397\u2192\n   398\u2192\tif sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.NumNodes() == 0 {\n   399\u2192\t\treturn result, ErrNoNodesAvailable\n   400\u2192\t}\n   401\u2192\n   402\u2192\tfeasibleNodes, diagnosis, err := sched.findNodesThatFitPod(ctx, fwk, state, pod)\n   403\u2192\tif err != nil {\n   404\u2192\t\treturn result, err\n   405\u2192\t}\n   406\u2192\ttrace.Step(\"Computing predicates done\")\n   407\u2192\n   408\u2192\tif len(feasibleNodes) == 0 {\n   409\u2192\t\treturn result, &framework.FitError{\n   410\u2192\t\t\tPod:         pod,\n   411\u2192\t\t\tNumAllNodes: sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.NumNodes(),\n   412\u2192\t\t\tDiagnosis:   diagnosis,\n   413\u2192\t\t}\n   414\u2192\t}\n   415\u2192\n   416\u2192\t// When only one node after predicate, just use it.\n   417\u2192\tif len(feasibleNodes) == 1 {\n   418\u2192\t\treturn ScheduleResult{\n   419\u2192\t\t\tSuggestedHost:  feasibleNodes[0].Node().Name,\n   420\u2192\t\t\tEvaluatedNodes: 1 + len(diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap),\n   421\u2192\t\t\tFeasibleNodes:  1,\n   422\u2192\t\t}, nil\n   423\u2192\t}\n   424\u2192\n   425\u2192\tpriorityList, err := prioritizeNodes(ctx, sched.Extenders, fwk, state, pod, feasibleNodes)\n   426\u2192\tif err != nil {\n   427\u2192\t\treturn result, err\n   428\u2192\t}\n   429\u2192\n   430\u2192\thost, _, err := selectHost(priorityList, numberOfHighestScoredNodesToReport)\n   431\u2192\ttrace.Step(\"Prioritizing done\")\n   432\u2192\n   433\u2192\treturn ScheduleResult{\n   434\u2192\t\tSuggestedHost:  host,\n   435\u2192\t\tEvaluatedNodes: len(feasibleNodes) + len(diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap),\n   436\u2192\t\tFeasibleNodes:  len(feasibleNodes),\n   437\u2192\t}, err\n   438\u2192}\n   439\u2192\n   440\u2192// Filters the nodes to find the ones that fit the pod based on the framework\n   441\u2192// filter plugins and filter extenders.\n   442\u2192func (sched *Scheduler) findNodesThatFitPod(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, state *framework.CycleState, pod *v1.Pod) ([]*framework.NodeInfo, framework.Diagnosis, error) {\n   443\u2192\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   444\u2192\tdiagnosis := framework.Diagnosis{\n   445\u2192\t\tNodeToStatusMap: make(framework.NodeToStatusMap),\n   446\u2192\t}\n   447\u2192\n   448\u2192\tallNodes, err := sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.NodeInfos().List()\n   449\u2192\tif err != nil {\n   450\u2192\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, err\n   451\u2192\t}\n   452\u2192\t// Run \"prefilter\" plugins.\n   453\u2192\tpreRes, s := fwk.RunPreFilterPlugins(ctx, state, pod)\n   454\u2192\tif !s.IsSuccess() {\n   455\u2192\t\tif !s.IsRejected() {\n   456\u2192\t\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, s.AsError()\n   457\u2192\t\t}\n   458\u2192\t\t// All nodes in NodeToStatusMap will have the same status so that they can be handled in the preemption.\n   459\u2192\t\t// Some non trivial refactoring is needed to avoid this copy.\n   460\u2192\t\tfor _, n := range allNodes {\n   461\u2192\t\t\tdiagnosis.NodeToStatusMap[n.Node().Name] = s\n   462\u2192\t\t}\n   463\u2192\n   464\u2192\t\t// Record the messages from PreFilter in Diagnosis.PreFilterMsg.\n   465\u2192\t\tmsg := s.Message()\n   466\u2192\t\tdiagnosis.PreFilterMsg = msg\n   467\u2192\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Status after running PreFilter plugins for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"status\", msg)\n   468\u2192\t\tdiagnosis.AddPluginStatus(s)\n   469\u2192\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, nil\n   470\u2192\t}\n   471\u2192\n   472\u2192\t// \"NominatedNodeName\" can potentially be set in a previous scheduling cycle as a result of preemption.\n   473\u2192\t// This node is likely the only candidate that will fit the pod, and hence we try it first before iterating over all nodes.\n   474\u2192\tif len(pod.Status.NominatedNodeName) > 0 {\n   475\u2192\t\tfeasibleNodes, err := sched.evaluateNominatedNode(ctx, pod, fwk, state, diagnosis)\n   476\u2192\t\tif err != nil {\n   477\u2192\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Evaluation failed on nominated node\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"node\", pod.Status.NominatedNodeName)\n   478\u2192\t\t}\n   479\u2192\t\t// Nominated node passes all the filters, scheduler is good to assign this node to the pod.\n   480\u2192\t\tif len(feasibleNodes) != 0 {\n   481\u2192\t\t\treturn feasibleNodes, diagnosis, nil\n   482\u2192\t\t}\n   483\u2192\t}\n   484\u2192\n   485\u2192\tnodes := allNodes\n   486\u2192\tif !preRes.AllNodes() {\n   487\u2192\t\tnodes = make([]*framework.NodeInfo, 0, len(preRes.NodeNames))\n   488\u2192\t\tfor _, n := range allNodes {\n   489\u2192\t\t\tif !preRes.NodeNames.Has(n.Node().Name) {\n   490\u2192\t\t\t\t// We consider Nodes that are filtered out by PreFilterResult as rejected via UnschedulableAndUnresolvable.\n   491\u2192\t\t\t\t// We have to record them in NodeToStatusMap so that they won't be considered as candidates in the preemption.\n   492\u2192\t\t\t\tdiagnosis.NodeToStatusMap[n.Node().Name] = framework.NewStatus(framework.UnschedulableAndUnresolvable, \"node is filtered out by the prefilter result\")\n   493\u2192\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   494\u2192\t\t\t}\n   495\u2192\t\t\tnodes = append(nodes, n)\n   496\u2192\t\t}\n   497\u2192\t}\n   498\u2192\tfeasibleNodes, err := sched.findNodesThatPassFilters(ctx, fwk, state, pod, &diagnosis, nodes)\n   499\u2192\t// always try to update the sched.nextStartNodeIndex regardless of whether an error has occurred\n   500\u2192\t// this is helpful to make sure that all the nodes have a chance to be searched\n   501\u2192\tprocessedNodes := len(feasibleNodes) + len(diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap)\n   502\u2192\tsched.nextStartNodeIndex = (sched.nextStartNodeIndex + processedNodes) % len(nodes)\n   503\u2192\tif err != nil {\n   504\u2192\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, err\n   505\u2192\t}\n   506\u2192\n   507\u2192\tfeasibleNodesAfterExtender, err := findNodesThatPassExtenders(ctx, sched.Extenders, pod, feasibleNodes, diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap)\n   508\u2192\tif err != nil {\n   509\u2192\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, err\n   510\u2192\t}\n   511\u2192\tif len(feasibleNodesAfterExtender) != len(feasibleNodes) {\n   512\u2192\t\t// Extenders filtered out some nodes.\n   513\u2192\t\t//\n   514\u2192\t\t// Extender doesn't support any kind of requeueing feature like EnqueueExtensions in the scheduling framework.\n   515\u2192\t\t// When Extenders reject some Nodes and the pod ends up being unschedulable,\n   516\u2192\t\t// we put framework.ExtenderName to pInfo.UnschedulablePlugins.\n   517\u2192\t\t// This Pod will be requeued from unschedulable pod pool to activeQ/backoffQ\n   518\u2192\t\t// by any kind of cluster events.\n   519\u2192\t\t// https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/122019\n   520\u2192\t\tif diagnosis.UnschedulablePlugins == nil {\n   521\u2192\t\t\tdiagnosis.UnschedulablePlugins = sets.New[string]()\n   522\u2192\t\t}\n   523\u2192\t\tdiagnosis.UnschedulablePlugins.Insert(framework.ExtenderName)\n   524\u2192\t}\n   525\u2192\n   526\u2192\treturn feasibleNodesAfterExtender, diagnosis, nil\n   527\u2192}\n   528\u2192\n   529\u2192func (sched *Scheduler) evaluateNominatedNode(ctx context.Context, pod *v1.Pod, fwk framework.Framework, state *framework.CycleState, diagnosis framework.Diagnosis) ([]*framework.NodeInfo, error) {\n   530\u2192\tnnn := pod.Status.NominatedNodeName\n   531\u2192\tnodeInfo, err := sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.Get(nnn)\n   532\u2192\tif err != nil {\n   533\u2192\t\treturn nil, err\n   534\u2192\t}\n   535\u2192\tnode := []*framework.NodeInfo{nodeInfo}\n   536\u2192\tfeasibleNodes, err := sched.findNodesThatPassFilters(ctx, fwk, state, pod, &diagnosis, node)\n   537\u2192\tif err != nil {\n   538\u2192\t\treturn nil, err\n   539\u2192\t}\n   540\u2192\n   541\u2192\tfeasibleNodes, err = findNodesThatPassExtenders(ctx, sched.Extenders, pod, feasibleNodes, diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap)\n   542\u2192\tif err != nil {\n   543\u2192\t\treturn nil, err\n   544\u2192\t}\n   545\u2192\n   546\u2192\treturn feasibleNodes, nil\n   547\u2192}\n   548\u2192\n   549\u2192// hasScoring checks if scoring nodes is configured.\n   550\u2192func (sched *Scheduler) hasScoring(fwk framework.Framework) bool {\n   551\u2192\tif fwk.HasScorePlugins() {\n   552\u2192\t\treturn true\n   553\u2192\t}\n   554\u2192\tfor _, extender := range sched.Extenders {\n   555\u2192\t\tif extender.IsPrioritizer() {\n   556\u2192\t\t\treturn true\n   557\u2192\t\t}\n   558\u2192\t}\n   559\u2192\treturn false\n   560\u2192}\n   561\u2192\n   562\u2192// hasExtenderFilters checks if any extenders filter nodes.\n   563\u2192func (sched *Scheduler) hasExtenderFilters() bool {\n   564\u2192\tfor _, extender := range sched.Extenders {\n   565\u2192\t\tif extender.IsFilter() {\n   566\u2192\t\t\treturn true\n   567\u2192\t\t}\n   568\u2192\t}\n   569\u2192\treturn false\n   570\u2192}\n   571\u2192\n   572\u2192// findNodesThatPassFilters finds the nodes that fit the filter plugins.\n   573\u2192func (sched *Scheduler) findNodesThatPassFilters(\n   574\u2192\tctx context.Context,\n   575\u2192\tfwk framework.Framework,\n   576\u2192\tstate *framework.CycleState,\n   577\u2192\tpod *v1.Pod,\n   578\u2192\tdiagnosis *framework.Diagnosis,\n   579\u2192\tnodes []*framework.NodeInfo) ([]*framework.NodeInfo, error) {\n   580\u2192\tnumAllNodes := len(nodes)\n   581\u2192\tnumNodesToFind := sched.numFeasibleNodesToFind(fwk.PercentageOfNodesToScore(), int32(numAllNodes))\n   582\u2192\tif !sched.hasExtenderFilters() && !sched.hasScoring(fwk) {\n   583\u2192\t\tnumNodesToFind = 1\n   584\u2192\t}\n   585\u2192\n   586\u2192\t// Create feasible list with enough space to avoid growing it\n   587\u2192\t// and allow assigning.\n   588\u2192\tfeasibleNodes := make([]*framework.NodeInfo, numNodesToFind)\n   589\u2192\n   590\u2192\tif !fwk.HasFilterPlugins() {\n   591\u2192\t\tfor i := range feasibleNodes {\n   592\u2192\t\t\tfeasibleNodes[i] = nodes[(sched.nextStartNodeIndex+i)%numAllNodes]\n   593\u2192\t\t}\n   594\u2192\t\treturn feasibleNodes, nil\n   595\u2192\t}\n   596\u2192\n   597\u2192\terrCh := parallelize.NewErrorChannel()\n   598\u2192\tvar feasibleNodesLen int32\n   599\u2192\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(ctx)\n   600\u2192\tdefer cancel()\n   601\u2192\n   602\u2192\ttype nodeStatus struct {\n   603\u2192\t\tnode   string\n   604\u2192\t\tstatus *framework.Status\n   605\u2192\t}\n   606\u2192\tresult := make([]*nodeStatus, numAllNodes)\n   607\u2192\tcheckNode := func(i int) {\n   608\u2192\t\t// We check the nodes starting from where we left off in the previous scheduling cycle,\n   609\u2192\t\t// this is to make sure all nodes have the same chance of being examined across pods.\n   610\u2192\t\tnodeInfo := nodes[(sched.nextStartNodeIndex+i)%numAllNodes]\n   611\u2192\t\tstatus := fwk.RunFilterPluginsWithNominatedPods(ctx, state, pod, nodeInfo)\n   612\u2192\t\tif status.Code() == framework.Error {\n   613\u2192\t\t\terrCh.SendErrorWithCancel(status.AsError(), cancel)\n   614\u2192\t\t\treturn\n   615\u2192\t\t}\n   616\u2192\t\tif status.IsSuccess() {\n   617\u2192\t\t\tlength := atomic.AddInt32(&feasibleNodesLen, 1)\n   618\u2192\t\t\tif length > numNodesToFind {\n   619\u2192\t\t\t\tcancel()\n   620\u2192\t\t\t\tatomic.AddInt32(&feasibleNodesLen, -1)\n   621\u2192\t\t\t} else {\n   622\u2192\t\t\t\tfeasibleNodes[length-1] = nodeInfo\n   623\u2192\t\t\t}\n   624\u2192\t\t} else {\n   625\u2192\t\t\tresult[i] = &nodeStatus{node: nodeInfo.Node().Name, status: status}\n   626\u2192\t\t}\n   627\u2192\t}\n   628\u2192\n   629\u2192\tbeginCheckNode := time.Now()\n   630\u2192\tstatusCode := framework.Success\n   631\u2192\tdefer func() {\n   632\u2192\t\t// We record Filter extension point latency here instead of in framework.go because framework.RunFilterPlugins\n   633\u2192\t\t// function is called for each node, whereas we want to have an overall latency for all nodes per scheduling cycle.\n   634\u2192\t\t// Note that this latency also includes latency for `addNominatedPods`, which calls framework.RunPreFilterAddPod.\n   635\u2192\t\tmetrics.FrameworkExtensionPointDuration.WithLabelValues(metrics.Filter, statusCode.String(), fwk.ProfileName()).Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(beginCheckNode))\n   636\u2192\t}()\n   637\u2192\n   638\u2192\t// Stops searching for more nodes once the configured number of feasible nodes\n   639\u2192\t// are found.\n   640\u2192\tfwk.Parallelizer().Until(ctx, numAllNodes, checkNode, metrics.Filter)\n   641\u2192\tfeasibleNodes = feasibleNodes[:feasibleNodesLen]\n   642\u2192\tfor _, item := range result {\n   643\u2192\t\tif item == nil {\n   644\u2192\t\t\tcontinue\n   645\u2192\t\t}\n   646\u2192\t\tdiagnosis.NodeToStatusMap[item.node] = item.status\n   647\u2192\t\tdiagnosis.AddPluginStatus(item.status)\n   648\u2192\t}\n   649\u2192\tif err := errCh.ReceiveError(); err != nil {\n   650\u2192\t\tstatusCode = framework.Error\n   651\u2192\t\treturn feasibleNodes, err\n   652\u2192\t}\n   653\u2192\treturn feasibleNodes, nil\n   654\u2192}\n   655\u2192\n   656\u2192// numFeasibleNodesToFind returns the number of feasible nodes that once found, the scheduler stops\n   657\u2192// its search for more feasible nodes.\n   658\u2192func (sched *Scheduler) numFeasibleNodesToFind(percentageOfNodesToScore *int32, numAllNodes int32) (numNodes int32) {\n   659\u2192\tif numAllNodes < minFeasibleNodesToFind {\n   660\u2192\t\treturn numAllNodes\n   661\u2192\t}\n   662\u2192\n   663\u2192\t// Use profile percentageOfNodesToScore if it's set. Otherwise, use global percentageOfNodesToScore.\n   664\u2192\tvar percentage int32\n   665\u2192\tif percentageOfNodesToScore != nil {\n   666\u2192\t\tpercentage = *percentageOfNodesToScore\n   667\u2192\t} else {\n   668\u2192\t\tpercentage = sched.percentageOfNodesToScore\n   669\u2192\t}\n   670\u2192\n   671\u2192\tif percentage == 0 {\n   672\u2192\t\tpercentage = int32(50) - numAllNodes/125\n   673\u2192\t\tif percentage < minFeasibleNodesPercentageToFind {\n   674\u2192\t\t\tpercentage = minFeasibleNodesPercentageToFind\n   675\u2192\t\t}\n   676\u2192\t}\n   677\u2192\n   678\u2192\tnumNodes = numAllNodes * percentage / 100\n   679\u2192\tif numNodes < minFeasibleNodesToFind {\n   680\u2192\t\treturn minFeasibleNodesToFind\n   681\u2192\t}\n   682\u2192\n   683\u2192\treturn numNodes\n   684\u2192}\n   685\u2192\n   686\u2192func findNodesThatPassExtenders(ctx context.Context, extenders []framework.Extender, pod *v1.Pod, feasibleNodes []*framework.NodeInfo, statuses framework.NodeToStatusMap) ([]*framework.NodeInfo, error) {\n   687\u2192\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   688\u2192\t// Extenders are called sequentially.\n   689\u2192\t// Nodes in original feasibleNodes can be excluded in one extender, and pass on to the next\n   690\u2192\t// extender in a decreasing manner.\n   691\u2192\tfor _, extender := range extenders {\n   692\u2192\t\tif len(feasibleNodes) == 0 {\n   693\u2192\t\t\tbreak\n   694\u2192\t\t}\n   695\u2192\t\tif !extender.IsInterested(pod) {\n   696\u2192\t\t\tcontinue\n   697\u2192\t\t}\n   698\u2192\n   699\u2192\t\t// Status of failed nodes in failedAndUnresolvableMap will be added or overwritten in <statuses>,\n   700\u2192\t\t// so that the scheduler framework can respect the UnschedulableAndUnresolvable status for\n   701\u2192\t\t// particular nodes, and this may eventually improve preemption efficiency.\n   702\u2192\t\t// Note: users are recommended to configure the extenders that may return UnschedulableAndUnresolvable\n   703\u2192\t\t// status ahead of others.\n   704\u2192\t\tfeasibleList, failedMap, failedAndUnresolvableMap, err := extender.Filter(pod, feasibleNodes)\n   705\u2192\t\tif err != nil {\n   706\u2192\t\t\tif extender.IsIgnorable() {\n   707\u2192\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Skipping extender as it returned error and has ignorable flag set\", \"extender\", extender, \"err\", err)\n   708\u2192\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   709\u2192\t\t\t}\n   710\u2192\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   711\u2192\t\t}\n   712\u2192\n   713\u2192\t\tfor failedNodeName, failedMsg := range failedAndUnresolvableMap {\n   714\u2192\t\t\tvar aggregatedReasons []string\n   715\u2192\t\t\tif _, found := statuses[failedNodeName]; found {\n   716\u2192\t\t\t\taggregatedReasons = statuses[failedNodeName].Reasons()\n   717\u2192\t\t\t}\n   718\u2192\t\t\taggregatedReasons = append(aggregatedReasons, failedMsg)\n   719\u2192\t\t\tstatuses[failedNodeName] = framework.NewStatus(framework.UnschedulableAndUnresolvable, aggregatedReasons...)\n   720\u2192\t\t}\n   721\u2192\n   722\u2192\t\tfor failedNodeName, failedMsg := range failedMap {\n   723\u2192\t\t\tif _, found := failedAndUnresolvableMap[failedNodeName]; found {\n   724\u2192\t\t\t\t// failedAndUnresolvableMap takes precedence over failedMap\n   725\u2192\t\t\t\t// note that this only happens if the extender returns the node in both maps\n   726\u2192\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   727\u2192\t\t\t}\n   728\u2192\t\t\tif _, found := statuses[failedNodeName]; !found {\n   729\u2192\t\t\t\tstatuses[failedNodeName] = framework.NewStatus(framework.Unschedulable, failedMsg)\n   730\u2192\t\t\t} else {\n   731\u2192\t\t\t\tstatuses[failedNodeName].AppendReason(failedMsg)\n   732\u2192\t\t\t}\n   733\u2192\t\t}\n   734\u2192\n   735\u2192\t\tfeasibleNodes = feasibleList\n   736\u2192\t}\n   737\u2192\treturn feasibleNodes, nil\n   738\u2192}\n   739\u2192\n   740\u2192// prioritizeNodes prioritizes the nodes by running the score plugins,\n   741\u2192// which return a score for each node from the call to RunScorePlugins().\n   742\u2192// The scores from each plugin are added together to make the score for that node, then\n   743\u2192// any extenders are run as well.\n   744\u2192// All scores are finally combined (added) to get the total weighted scores of all nodes\n   745\u2192func prioritizeNodes(\n   746\u2192\tctx context.Context,\n   747\u2192\textenders []framework.Extender,\n   748\u2192\tfwk framework.Framework,\n   749\u2192\tstate *framework.CycleState,\n   750\u2192\tpod *v1.Pod,\n   751\u2192\tnodes []*framework.NodeInfo,\n   752\u2192) ([]framework.NodePluginScores, error) {\n   753\u2192\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   754\u2192\t// If no priority configs are provided, then all nodes will have a score of one.\n   755\u2192\t// This is required to generate the priority list in the required format\n   756\u2192\tif len(extenders) == 0 && !fwk.HasScorePlugins() {\n   757\u2192\t\tresult := make([]framework.NodePluginScores, 0, len(nodes))\n   758\u2192\t\tfor i := range nodes {\n   759\u2192\t\t\tresult = append(result, framework.NodePluginScores{\n   760\u2192\t\t\t\tName:       nodes[i].Node().Name,\n   761\u2192\t\t\t\tTotalScore: 1,\n   762\u2192\t\t\t})\n   763\u2192\t\t}\n   764\u2192\t\treturn result, nil\n   765\u2192\t}\n   766\u2192\n   767\u2192\t// Run PreScore plugins.\n   768\u2192\tpreScoreStatus := fwk.RunPreScorePlugins(ctx, state, pod, nodes)\n   769\u2192\tif !preScoreStatus.IsSuccess() {\n   770\u2192\t\treturn nil, preScoreStatus.AsError()\n   771\u2192\t}\n   772\u2192\n   773\u2192\t// Run the Score plugins.\n   774\u2192\tnodesScores, scoreStatus := fwk.RunScorePlugins(ctx, state, pod, nodes)\n   775\u2192\tif !scoreStatus.IsSuccess() {\n   776\u2192\t\treturn nil, scoreStatus.AsError()\n   777\u2192\t}\n   778\u2192\n   779\u2192\t// Additional details logged at level 10 if enabled.\n   780\u2192\tloggerVTen := logger.V(10)\n   781\u2192\tif loggerVTen.Enabled() {\n   782\u2192\t\tfor _, nodeScore := range nodesScores {\n   783\u2192\t\t\tfor _, pluginScore := range nodeScore.Scores {\n 1 // 1111111\n\n\t// Use the general Update type if you don't either know or care the specific sub-Update type to use.\n\tUpdate = UpdateNodeAllocatable | UpdateNodeLabel | UpdateNodeTaint | UpdateNodeCondition | UpdateNodeAnnotation\n)\n\n// GVK is short for group/version/kind, which can uniquely represent a particular API resource.\ntype GVK string\n\n// Constants for GVKs.\nconst (\n\t// There are a couple of notes about how the scheduler notifies the events of Pods:\n\t// - Add: add events could be triggered by either a newly created Pod or an existing Pod that is scheduled to a Node.\n\t// - Delete: delete events could be triggered by:\n\t//           - a Pod that is deleted\n\t//           - a Pod that was assumed, but gets un-assumed due to some errors in the binding cycle.\n\t//           - an existing Pod that was unscheduled but gets scheduled to a Node.\n\tPod GVK = \"Pod\"\n\t// A note about NodeAdd event and UpdateNodeTaint event:\n\t// NodeAdd QueueingHint isn't always called because of the internal feature called preCheck.\n\t// It's definitely not something expected for plugin developers,\n\t// and registering UpdateNodeTaint event is the only mitigation for now.\n\t// So, kube-scheduler registers UpdateNodeTaint event for plugins that has NodeAdded event, but don't have UpdateNodeTaint event.\n\t// It has a bad impact for the requeuing efficiency though, a lot better than some Pods being stuck in the\n\t// unschedulable pod pool.\n\t// This behavior will be removed when we remove the preCheck feature.\n\t// See: https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/110175\n\tNode                    GVK = \"Node\"\n\tPersistentVolume        GVK = \"PersistentVolume\"\n\tPersistentVolumeClaim   GVK = \"PersistentVolumeClaim\"\n\tCSINode                 GVK = \"storage.k8s.io/CSINode\"\n\tCSIDriver               GVK = \"storage.k8s.io/CSIDriver\"\n\tCSIStorageCapacity      GVK = \"storage.k8s.io/CSIStorageCapacity\"\n\tStorageClass            GVK = \"storage.k8s.io/StorageClass\"\n\tPodSchedulingContext    GVK = \"PodSchedulingContext\"\n\tResourceClaim           GVK = \"ResourceClaim\"\n\tResourceClass           GVK = \"ResourceClass\"\n\tResourceClaimParameters GVK = \"ResourceClaimParameters\"\n\tResourceClassParameters GVK = \"ResourceClassParameters\"\n\n\t// WildCard is a special GVK to match all resources.\n\t// e.g., If you register `{Resource: \"*\", ActionType: All}` in EventsToRegister,\n\t// all coming clusterEvents will be admitted. Be careful to register it, it will\n\t// increase the computing pressure in requeueing unless you really need it.\n\t//\n\t// Meanwhile, if the coming clusterEvent is a wildcard one, all pods\n\t// will be moved from unschedulablePod pool to activeQ/backoffQ forcibly.\n\tWildCard GVK = \"*\"\n)\n\ntype ClusterEventWithHint struct {\n\tEvent ClusterEvent\n\t// QueueingHintFn is executed for the plugin rejected by this plugin when the above Event happens,\n\t// and filters out events to reduce useless retry of Pod's scheduling.\n\t// It's an optional field. If not set,\n\t// the scheduling of Pods will be always retried with backoff when this Event happens.\n\t// (the same as Queue)\n\tQueueingHintFn QueueingHintFn\n}\n\n// QueueingHintFn returns a hint backoffQ or activeQ.\n// If it returns an error, we'll take the returned QueueingHint as `Queue` at the caller whatever we returned here so that\n// we can prevent the Pod from being stuck in the unschedulable pod pool.\n//\n// - `pod`: the Pod to be enqueued, which is rejected by this plugin in the past.\n// - `oldObj` `newObj`: the object involved in that event.\n//   - For example, the given event is \"Node deleted\", the `oldObj` will be that deleted Node.\n//   - `oldObj` is nil if the event is add event.\n//   - `newObj` is nil if the event is delete event.\ntype QueueingHintFn      string\n}\n\n// IsWildCard returns true if ClusterEvent follows WildCard semantics\nfunc (ce ClusterEvent) IsWildCard() bool {\n\treturn ce.Resource == WildCard && ce.ActionType == All\n}\n\n// *v1.Pod\n\tNumAllNodes int\n\tDiagnosis   Diagnosis\n}\n\nconst (\n\t// NoNodeAvailableMsg is used to format message when no nodes available.\n\tNoNodeAvailableMsg = \"0/%v nodes are available\"\n)\n\nfunc (d *Diagnosis) AddPluginStatus(sts *Status) {\n\tif sts.Plugin() == \"\" {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tif sts.IsRejected() {\n\t\tif d.UnschedulablePlugins == nil message format is \"0/X nodes are available: <PreFilterMsg>. <FilterMsg>. <PostFilterMsg>.\"\nfunc (f *FitError) Error() string {\n\treasonMsg := fmt.Sprintf(NoNodeAvailableMsg+\":\", f.NumAllNodes)\n\tpreFilterMsg := f.Diagnosis.PreFilterMsg\n\tif preFilterMsg != \"\" {\n\t\t// PreFilter plugin returns unschedulable.\n\t\t// Add the messages from PreFilter plugins to reasonMsg.\n\t\treasonMsg += fmt.Sprintf(\" %v.\", preFilterMsg)\n\t}\n\n\tif preFilterMsg == \"\" {\n\t\t// the scheduling cycle went through PreFilter extension point successfully.\n\t\t//\n\t\t// When the prefilter plugin returns unschedulable,\n\t\t// the scheduling framework inserts the same unschedulable status to all nodes in NodeToStatusMap.\n\t\t// So, we shouldn't add the message from NodeToStatusMap when the PreFilter failed.\n\t\t// Otherwise, we will have duplicated reasons in the error message.\n\t\treasons := make(map[string]int)\n\t\tfor _, status := range f.Diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap {\n\t\t\tfor _, reason := range status.Reasons() {\n\t\t\t\treasons[reason]++\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tsortReasonsHistogram := func() []string {\n\t\t\tvar reasonStrings []string\n\t\t\tfor k, v := range reasons {\n\t\t\t\treasonStrings = append(reasonStrings, fmt.Sprintf(\"%v %v\", v, k))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tsort.Strings(reasonStrings)\n\t\t\treturn reasonStrings\n\t\t}\n\t\tsortedFilterMsg := sortReasonsHistogram()\n\t\tif len(sortedFilterMsg) != 0 {\n\t\t\treasonMsg += fmt.Sprintf(\" %v.\", strings.Join(sortedFilterMsg, \", \"))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Add the messages from PostFilter plugins to reasonMsg.\n\t// We can add this message regardless of whether the scheduling cycle fails at PreFilter or Filter\n\t// since we may run PostFilter (if enabled) in both cases.\n\tpostFilterMsg := f.Diagnosis.PostFilterMsg\n\tif postFilterMsg != \"\" {\n\t\treasonMsg += fmt.Sprintf(\" %v\", postFilterMsg)\n\t}\n\treturn reasonMsg\n}\n\nfunc newAffinityTerm(pod *v1.Pod, term *v1.PodAffinityTerm) (*AffinityTerm, error) {\n\tselector, err := metav1.LabelSelectorAsSelector(term.LabelSelector)\n\tif err != nil   "content": "# Kubernetes Scheduler: Missing ResourceSlice Event Handler Bug Analysis\n\n## Files Examined\n- `pkg/scheduler/schedule_one.go` \u2014 Entry point for pod scheduling; implements the scheduling cycle that invokes plugins\n- `pkg/scheduler/eventhandlers.go` \u2014 Registers event handlers for cluster resource changes; handles Pod, Node, Storage, and DRA-related resources\n- `pkg/scheduler/framework/types.go` \u2014 Defines GVK (Group/Version/Kind) constants for all resources that trigger scheduling queue re-evaluation\n- `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/dynamicresources/dynamicresources.go` \u2014 DRA plugin that validates pod resource claims; uses ResourceSliceLister but does NOT register ResourceSlice events\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1alpha2/types.go` \u2014 Defines ResourceSlice API type; used by DRA drivers to advertise available resources\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/informers/resource/v1alpha2/interface.go` \u2014 SharedInformerFactory provides ResourceSlices() method for accessing ResourceSlice informer\n\n## Dependency Chain\n1. **Symptom observed in**: `pkg/scheduler/schedule_one.go:ScheduleOne()`\n   - Pod requesting DRA devices arrives at scheduler\n   - Plugin execution reaches dynamicresources plugin PreFilter phase\n\n2. **Called from**: `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/dynamicresources/dynamicresources.go:EventsToRegister()`\n   - Plugin declares which events should trigger pod re-evaluation\n   - RegisterResourceClaim, ResourceClass, PodSchedulingContext, etc. events registered\n   - **BUT ResourceSlice events are NOT registered** (missing line)\n\n3. **Propagated to**: `pkg/scheduler/scheduler.go:unionedGVKs()`\n   - Collects all GVKs from all plugins' EventsToRegister()\n   - Builds gvkMap: `map[framework.GVK]framework.ActionType`\n   - ResourceSlice GVK never added because plugin didn't request it\n\n4. **Passed to**: `pkg/scheduler/eventhandlers.go:addAllEventHandlers()`\n   - Iterates through gvkMap to register informer event handlers\n   - For each GVK, adds handler to move unschedulable pods to active/backoff queue on events\n   - **No case for ResourceSlice in switch statement** (lines 396-542)\n\n5. **Bug triggered by**: `pkg/scheduler/framework/types.go` lines 68-106\n   - **ResourceSlice GVK constant is NOT DEFINED**\n   - Means plugins cannot register ResourceSlice events structurally\n   - UnrollWildCardResource() (lines 177-193) also missing ResourceSlice\n\n## Root Cause\n\n**File**: `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/dynamicresources/dynamicresources.go`\n\n**Function**: `EventsToRegister()` (approximately line 1215-1240)\n\n**Line**: Missing code block (should exist but doesn't)\n\n**Explanation**:\nThe dynamicresources plugin has three critical issues:\n\n1. **Missing Event Registration**: The plugin's `EventsToRegister()` method registers events for ResourceClaim, ResourceClass, PodSchedulingContext, ResourceClaimParameters, and ResourceClassParameters, but **does NOT include ResourceSlice** events. This is the direct cause of the bug.\n\n2. **ResourceSlice Not in Framework**: The `framework/types.go` file defines GVK constants for other DRA resources (ResourceClaim, ResourceClass, ResourceClaimParameters, ResourceClassParameters, PodSchedulingContext) but **ResourceSlice is missing**. This blocks the ability to register the event handler.\n\n3. **Event Handler Not Implemented**: The `eventhandlers.go` file has a case for PodSchedulingContext (line 448), ResourceClaim (line 457), ResourceClass (line 466), ResourceClaimParameters (line 475), and ResourceClassParameters (line 484), but **no case for ResourceSlice**. Even if a plugin tried to register the event, the scheduler wouldn't know how to attach the event handler to the ResourceSlice informer.\n\n**Why This Causes the Bug**:\n- When a pod requesting DRA devices is scheduled before the DRA driver publishes ResourceSlices, the dynamicresources plugin's Filter hook returns `Unschedulable` because `structuredParameters.go:newResourceModel()` cannot find any ResourceSlices to validate available resources\n- The pod is added to the unschedulable queue with the assumption that a future event will trigger re-evaluation\n- Later, when the DRA driver publishes ResourceSlice objects, there is NO event handler listening to ResourceSlice changes\n- No ClusterEvent is generated, so pods waiting in the unschedulable queue are never re-queued\n- **The pod remains stuck permanently in Unschedulable state**\n\n## Proposed Fix\n\n### Fix 1: Add ResourceSlice GVK to framework/types.go\n\n```diff\n// pkg/scheduler/framework/types.go (after line 96)\n\nconst (\n\t// ... existing constants ...\n\tResourceClass           GVK = \"ResourceClass\"\n\tResourceClaimParameters GVK = \"ResourceClaimParameters\"\n\tResourceClassParameters GVK = \"ResourceClassParameters\"\n+\tResourceSlice           GVK = \"ResourceSlice\"\n\n\t// WildCard is a special GVK to match all resources.\n```\n\n### Fix 2: Add ResourceSlice to UnrollWildCardResource() in framework/types.go\n\n```diff\n// pkg/scheduler/framework/types.go (in UnrollWildCardResource function)\n\nfunc UnrollWildCardResource() []ClusterEventWithHint {\n\treturn []ClusterEventWithHint{\n\t\t// ... existing events ...\n\t\t{Event: ClusterEvent{Resource: ResourceClaimParameters, ActionType: All}},\n\t\t{Event: ClusterEvent{Resource: ResourceClassParameters, ActionType: All}},\n+\t\t{Event: ClusterEvent{Resource: ResourceSlice, ActionType: All}},\n\t}\n}\n```\n\n### Fix 3: Add ResourceSlice event handler to eventhandlers.go\n\n```diff\n// pkg/scheduler/eventhandlers.go (in addAllEventHandlers function, after ResourceClassParameters case at line 492)\n\n\t\tcase framework.ResourceClassParameters:\n\t\t\tif utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {\n\t\t\t\tif handlerRegistration, err = informerFactory.Resource().V1alpha2().ResourceClassParameters().Informer().AddEventHandler(\n\t\t\t\t\tbuildEvtResHandler(at, framework.ResourceClassParameters, \"ResourceClassParameters\"),\n\t\t\t\t); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\thandlers = append(handlers, handlerRegistration)\n\t\t\t}\n+\t\tcase framework.ResourceSlice:\n+\t\t\tif utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {\n+\t\t\t\tif handlerRegistration, err = informerFactory.Resource().V1alpha2().ResourceSlices().Informer().AddEventHandler(\n+\t\t\t\t\tbuildEvtResHandler(at, framework.ResourceSlice, \"ResourceSlice\"),\n+\t\t\t\t); err != nil {\n+\t\t\t\t\treturn err\n+\t\t\t\t}\n+\t\t\t\thandlers = append(handlers, handlerRegistration)\n+\t\t\t}\n\t\tcase framework.StorageClass:\n```\n\n### Fix 4: Add ResourceSlice events to dynamicresources plugin EventsToRegister() in dynamicresources.go\n\n```diff\n// pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/dynamicresources/dynamicresources.go (in EventsToRegister method)\n\nfunc (pl *dynamicResources) EventsToRegister() []framework.ClusterEventWithHint {\n\tif !pl.enabled {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tevents := []framework.ClusterEventWithHint{\n\t\t// ... existing events ...\n\t\t{Event: framework.ClusterEvent{Resource: framework.ResourceClass, ActionType: framework.Add | framework.Update}},\n+\t\t// ResourceSlices published by DRA drivers may make pods schedulable by providing capacity information.\n+\t\t{Event: framework.ClusterEvent{Resource: framework.ResourceSlice, ActionType: framework.Add | framework.Update}, QueueingHintFn: pl.isSchedulableAfterResourceSliceChange},\n\t}\n\treturn events\n}\n```\n\nAnd add the corresponding QueueingHintFn:\n\n```diff\n// Add this method to the dynamicResources plugin struct\n\n+// isSchedulableAfterResourceSliceChange is invoked for add and update resource slice events.\n+// It checks whether that change made a previously unschedulable pod schedulable.\n+// It errs on the side of letting a pod scheduling attempt happen.\n+func (pl *dynamicResources) isSchedulableAfterResourceSliceChange(logger klog.Logger, pod *v1.Pod, oldObj, newObj interface{}) (framework.QueueingHint, error) {\n+\t// Any ResourceSlice change might make a pod that uses structured parameters schedulable,\n+\t// so we should always retry.\n+\treturn framework.Queue, nil\n+}\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Execution Path from Symptom to Root Cause\n\n1. **Initial Scheduling Attempt** (pod created before DRA driver starts):\n   - Pod with ResourceClaim arrives at scheduler\n   - `schedule_one.go:ScheduleOne()` begins scheduling cycle\n   - Plugins execute PreFilter \u2192 Filter phases\n   - dynamicresources plugin's `Filter()` hook runs\n   - `structuredparameters.go:newResourceModel()` is called\n   - ResourceSliceLister has NO ResourceSlices (driver hasn't started)\n   - Plugin returns `Unschedulable` status: \"cannot allocate all claims\"\n   - Pod marked as unschedulable, moved to unschedulable queue\n\n2. **Pod Queued for Re-evaluation** (scheduling cycle completes):\n   - Pod has UnschedulablePlugins = {dynamicResources}\n   - Stored in scheduler's unschedulable pod pool\n   - Waits for a registered ClusterEvent to trigger re-evaluation\n\n3. **DRA Driver Starts** (driver publishes ResourceSlice):\n   - DRA driver creates ResourceSlice objects with available resources\n   - ResourceSlice objects appear in apiserver\n   - **ResourceSlice informer receives Add event**\n   - **BUT no event handler is registered for ResourceSlice**\n   - Event is silently dropped (not delivered to scheduler)\n\n4. **Pod Stays Stuck** (race condition manifests):\n   - No ClusterEvent is generated for ResourceSlice changes\n   - Scheduler never calls `MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue` for unschedulable pods\n   - Pod remains in unschedulable queue indefinitely\n   - Pod will never be retried unless another event (like Node change) happens\n\n### Why This is a Race Condition\n\n- **If driver starts FIRST**: ResourceSlices exist when pod arrives \u2192 dynamicresources plugin sees resources \u2192 scheduling succeeds\n- **If pod arrives FIRST**: No ResourceSlices exist \u2192 plugin marks pod unschedulable \u2192 driver starts and publishes ResourceSlices \u2192 but no event handler catches this \u2192 pod stuck forever\n\n### The Missing Link\n\nThe scheduler's event-driven architecture works like this:\n1. Plugins declare events they care about via `EventsToRegister()` \u2192 QueueingHintFn\n2. Scheduler registers event handlers for those events with informers\n3. When events fire, handlers call `MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue()` with appropriate QueueingHints\n4. Unschedulable pods matching QueueingHints are retried\n\nResourceSlice events were never added to this pipeline, so they never trigger pod re-evaluation.\n\n## Impact\n\nThis bug prevents Dynamic Resource Allocation (DRA) from functioning in production scenarios where:\n- DRA drivers (like GPU device plugins) start after user pods\n- Pods request resources via ResourceClaim objects\n- Pods become permanently stuck if scheduling is attempted before driver publishes ResourceSlices\n\nThe fix ensures that whenever a DRA driver publishes or updates ResourceSlices, pods waiting for those resources are immediately re-evaluated for scheduling.\n",

  "originalFile": "# Kubernetes Scheduler: Missing ResourceSlice Event Handler Bug Analysis\n\n## Files Examined\n- `pkg/scheduler/schedule_one.go` \u2014 Entry point for pod scheduling; implements the scheduling cycle that invokes plugins\n- `pkg/scheduler/eventhandlers.go` \u2014 Registers event handlers for cluster resource changes; handles Pod, Node, Storage, and DRA-related resources\n- `pkg/scheduler/framework/types.go` \u2014 Defines GVK (Group/Version/Kind) constants for all resources that trigger scheduling queue re-evaluation\n- `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/dynamicresources/dynamicresources.go` \u2014 DRA plugin that validates pod resource claims; uses ResourceSliceLister but does NOT register ResourceSlice events\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1alpha2/types.go` \u2014 Defines ResourceSlice API type; used by DRA drivers to advertise available resources\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/informers/resource/v1alpha2/interface.go` \u2014 SharedInformerFactory provides ResourceSlices() method for accessing ResourceSlice informer\n\n## Dependency Chain\n1. **Symptom observed in**: `pkg/scheduler/schedule_one.go:ScheduleOne()`\n   - Pod requesting DRA devices arrives at scheduler\n   - Plugin execution reaches dynamicresources plugin PreFilter phase\n\n2. **Called from**: `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/dynamicresources/dynamicresources.go:EventsToRegister()`\n   - Plugin declares which events should trigger pod re-evaluation\n   - RegisterResourceClaim, ResourceClass, PodSchedulingContext, etc. events registered\n   - **BUT ResourceSlice events are NOT registered** (missing line)\n\n3. **Propagated to**: `pkg/scheduler/scheduler.go:unionedGVKs()`\n   - Collects all GVKs from all plugins' EventsToRegister()\n   - Builds gvkMap: `map[framework.GVK]framework.ActionType`\n   - ResourceSlice GVK never added because plugin didn't request it\n\n4. **Passed to**: `pkg/scheduler/eventhandlers.go:addAllEventHandlers()`\n   - Iterates through gvkMap to register informer event handlers\n   - For each GVK, adds handler to move unschedulable pods to active/backoff queue on events\n   - **No case for ResourceSlice in switch statement** (lines 396-542)\n\n5. **Bug triggered by**: `pkg/scheduler/framework/types.go` lines 68-106\n   - **ResourceSlice GVK constant is NOT DEFINED**\n   - Means plugins cannot register ResourceSlice events structurally\n   - UnrollWildCardResource() (lines 177-193) also missing ResourceSlice\n\n## Root Cause\n\n**File**: `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/dynamicresources/dynamicresources.go`\n\n**Function**: `EventsToRegister()` (approximately line 1215-1240)\n\n**Line**: Missing code block (should exist but doesn't)\n\n**Explanation**:\nThe dynamicresources plugin has three critical issues:\n\n1. **Missing Event Registration**: The plugin's `EventsToRegister()` method registers events for ResourceClaim, ResourceClass, PodSchedulingContext, ResourceClaimParameters, and ResourceClassParameters, but **does NOT include ResourceSlice** events. This is the direct cause of the bug.\n\n2. **ResourceSlice Not in Framework**: The `framework/types.go` file defines GVK constants for other DRA resources (ResourceClaim, ResourceClass, ResourceClaimParameters, ResourceClassParameters, PodSchedulingContext) but **ResourceSlice is missing**. This blocks the ability to register the event handler.\n\n3. **Event Handler Not Implemented**: The `eventhandlers.go` file has a case for PodSchedulingContext (line 448), ResourceClaim (line 457), ResourceClass (line 466), ResourceClaimParameters (line 475), and ResourceClassParameters (line 484), but **no case for ResourceSlice**. Even if a plugin tried to register the event, the scheduler wouldn't know how to attach the event handler to the ResourceSlice informer.\n\n**Why This Causes the Bug**:\n- When a pod requesting DRA devices is scheduled before the DRA driver publishes ResourceSlices, the dynamicresources plugin's Filter hook returns `Unschedulable` because `structuredParameters.go:newResourceModel()` cannot find any ResourceSlices to validate available resources\n- The pod is added to the unschedulable queue with the assumption that a future event will trigger re-evaluation\n- Later, when the DRA driver publishes ResourceSlice objects, there is NO event handler listening to ResourceSlice changes\n- No ClusterEvent is generated, so pods waiting in the unschedulable queue are never re-queued\n- **The pod remains stuck permanently in Unschedulable state**\n\n## Proposed Fix\n\n### Fix 1: Add ResourceSlice GVK to framework/types.go\n\n```diff\n// pkg/scheduler/framework/types.go (after line error) {\n+\t// Any ResourceSlice change might make a pod that uses structured parameters schedulable,\n+\t// so we should always retry.\n+\treturn framework.Queue, nil\n+}\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Execution Path from Symptom to Root Cause\n\n1. **Initial Scheduling Attempt** (pod created before DRA driver starts):\n   - Pod with ResourceClaim arrives at scheduler\n   - `schedule_one.go:ScheduleOne()` begins scheduling cycle\n   - Plugins execute PreFilter \u2192 Filter phases\n   - dynamicresources plugin's `Filter()` hook runs\n   - `structuredparameters.go:newResourceModel()` is called\n   - ResourceSliceLister has NO ResourceSlices (driver hasn't started)\n   - Plugin returns `Unschedulable` status: \"cannot allocate all claims\"\n   - Pod marked as unschedulable, moved to unschedulable queue\n\n2. **Pod Queued for Re-evaluation** (scheduling cycle completes):\n   - Pod has UnschedulablePlugins = {dynamicResources}\n   - Stored in scheduler's unschedulable pod pool\n   - Waits for a registered ClusterEvent to trigger re-evaluation\n\n3. **DRA Driver Starts** (driver publishes ResourceSlice):\n   - DRA driver creates ResourceSlice objects with available resources\n   - ResourceSlice objects appear in apiserver\n   - **ResourceSlice informer receives Add event**\n   - **BUT no event handler is registered for ResourceSlice**\n   - Event is silently dropped (not delivered to scheduler)\n\n4. **Pod Stays Stuck** (race condition manifests):\n   - No ClusterEvent is generated for ResourceSlice changes\n   - Scheduler never calls `MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue` for unschedulable pods\n   - Pod remains in unschedulable queue indefinitely\n   - Pod will never be retried unless another event (like Node change) happens\n\n### Why This is a Race Condition\n\n- **If driver starts FIRST**: ResourceSlices exist when pod arrives \u2192 dynamicresources plugin sees resources \u2192 scheduling succeeds\n- **If pod arrives FIRST**: No ResourceSlices exist \u2192 plugin marks pod unschedulable \u2192 driver starts and publishes ResourceSlices \u2192 but no event handler catches this \u2192 pod stuck forever\n\n### The Missing Link\n\nThe scheduler's event-driven architecture works like this:\n1. Plugins declare events they care about via `EventsToRegister()` \u2192 QueueingHintFn\n2. Scheduler registers event handlers for those events with informers\n3. When events fire, handlers call `MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue()` with appropriate QueueingHints\n4. Unschedulable pods matching QueueingHints are retried\n\nResourceSlice events were never added to this pipeline, so they never trigger pod re-evaluation.\n\n## Impact\n\nThis bug prevents Dynamic Resource Allocation (DRA) from functioning in production scenarios where:\n- DRA drivers (like GPU device plugins) start after user pods\n- Pods request resources via ResourceClaim objects\n- Pods become permanently stuck if scheduling is attempted before driver publishes ResourceSlices\n\nThe fix ensures that whenever a DRA driver publishes or updates ResourceSlices, pods waiting for those resources are immediately re-evaluated for scheduling.\n",
